最新的推理结果的根原因位点现在的报警状态如何？	select t_rt_data.Alarm_status from t_rt_data where t_rt_data.Tag_code = ( select t_inference_data.Inference_root_cause_id from t_inference_data order by t_inference_data.Id desc limit 1 ) order by t_rt_data.Id desc limit 1 ;
查看诊断结果表中最后一条记录的根原因变量在实时数据库中最近的报警状态。	select t_rt_data.Alarm_status from t_rt_data where t_rt_data.Tag_code = ( select t_inference_data.Inference_root_cause_id from t_inference_data order by t_inference_data.Id desc limit 1 ) order by t_rt_data.Id desc limit 1 ;
统计进集合管原料温度的每个模型的路径在推理表中作为最优路径出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where t_model_data.Tag_code = '3B2CHLH_0202B_TI112F.PV' group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
统计分馏塔底油浆出口温度的每个模型的路径在推理表中作为最优路径出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where t_model_data.Tag_code = '3B1CHLH_TI336.PV' group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
在线推理表中燃烧油喷嘴上部温度的每个因果模型作为最优路径出现过多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where t_model_data.Tag_code = '3B1CHLH_TI228A.PV' group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
在线推理表中F205炉出口总温度的每个因果模型作为最优路径出现过多少次？	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where t_model_data.Tag_code = '2B2LXCZ_0211TIC_21512' group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
统计模型表中所有路径在推理表中最优路径一栏中出现的次数，按次数从少到多排列。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path order by count ( * ) asc ;
请帮我按照实时诊断表的最优路径一栏中出现的次数升序排列所有可能的路径。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path order by count ( * ) asc ;
哪些可能的推断路径在根原因推断的最优路径中出现过13次以上？	select t_model_data.Inference_path from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path having count ( * ) > 13 ;
哪些可能的推断路径在根原因推断的最优路径中出现过20次以上？	select t_model_data.Inference_path from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path having count ( * ) > 20 ;
统计那些被推断为最优路径11次以上的模型表中的推理路径。	select t_model_data.Inference_path from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path having count ( * ) > 11 ;
统计那些被推断为最优路径18次以上的模型表中的推理路径。	select t_model_data.Inference_path from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path group by t_model_data.Inference_path having count ( * ) > 18 ;
统计模型表中每条字符串长度小于14的模型路径在最近36小时内在根原因推断表的最优路径中出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 14 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 36 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
统计模型表中每条字符串长度小于15的模型路径在最近30小时内在根原因推断表的最优路径中出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 15 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 30 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
